# VERIFICATION.md вҖ” live-browser test checklist

Some changes pass every check we can run **without a browser** вҖ” `npm run lint`,
`npm test`, `npm run build`, and server-side endpoint calibration вҖ” but still need a
human (or a Claude coworker with a real browser) to confirm they actually work **in the
running app**. This file is the running list of those, so nothing that "builds green but
was never clicked" quietly ships broken.

> **Production app:** https://planyr.io (Cloudflare Pages, deploys from `main`).
> **This is the runtime counterpart to `BACKLOG.md`.** An item can be `[x]` done in the
> backlog and still вҸі unverified here вҖ” the code landed; the click-through hasn't.

> ## вҡ пёҸ Testing policy (updated 2026-06-17 вҖ” read this)
> **Michael does NOT click through to test things himself. Ever.** Don't wait on him, don't ask
> him to verify, don't end a turn expecting him to go look.
> **Claude self-verifies in a headless browser вҖ” in the same session, no separate "cohort."**
> A headless Chromium is available in the environment (see "рҹӨ– Self-verification" below), so a
> session that ships a UI change should **drive the live app itself** and record the result rather
> than file the click-through for someone else. The working rhythm:
> - After a change is **CI-green + build-green**, **run the headless-browser check yourself**, then
>   record the outcome here (вң…/вқҢ + date). Don't punt it.
> - **Only if no browser is reachable** (rare), log the item below and move on вҖ” never block on Michael.
> - **Do NOT surface "these N are unverified" to Michael as a to-do for him.**
> - **Only interrupt Michael for a genuinely CRITICAL problem** вҖ” the app won't build, won't render
>   (blank screen), or a shipped feature is visibly crashing in production. Everything else: note it
>   here, keep moving.
>
> ### рҹӨ– Self-verification вҖ” how (proven 2026-06-17 against planyr.io + per-branch preview URLs)
> Write a short Playwright script and run it with Node:
> - Browsers live at `PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH=/opt/pw-browsers`; the module is the global
>   `/opt/node22/lib/node_modules/playwright` (require it by absolute path).
> - The sandbox egress proxy intercepts TLS, so launch with `args:['--ignore-certificate-errors']`
>   **and** `newContext({ ignoreHTTPSErrors: true })`, or `page.goto` throws `ERR_CERT_AUTHORITY_INVALID`.
> - **Logged-out only:** that proxy also CORS-blocks the Supabase auth handshake, so self-tests run in
>   **this-device (logged-out) mode** вҖ” full coverage for the planner/drawing tools, but anything that
>   *requires* sign-in (cloud save/sync) still needs a signed-in check elsewhere.
> - Enter the planner via **"Start blank"**; drive the SVG canvas with `page.mouse` (CDP mouse events
>   fire React's pointer handlers); `page.screenshot({clip})` then read the PNG back to eyeball it.

---

## How to use this вҖ” Claude Code / coworkers, read on every run

1. **Scan the рҹ”І list below** вҖ” items waiting to be confirmed in the running app. Per the testing
   policy above, do **not** hand this list to Michael as his to-do; only escalate a **critical**
   (won't build / won't render / crashing) issue.
2. **Verify it yourself in a headless browser** (see "рҹӨ– Self-verification" above): run the
   **Steps**, compare to **Expect**, then record the outcome.
3. **вӣ” CLEAR OUT what you finish вҖ” don't leave passed items piling up here (owner rule, 2026-07-02).**
   This is the #1 reason this file bloats. Whoever runs a check (usually Claude Cowork on the live app вҖ”
   NOT Michael) archives it the SAME session, by item type:
   - **One-off item** (`Cadence: once` вҖ” a bug/feature acceptance check): once it **fully passes with
     nothing pending**, **MOVE its whole block to `VERIFICATION-DONE.md`** вҖ” do not just mark it вң… and
     leave it here. (Same archiving discipline as `BACKLOG.md вҶ’ BACKLOG-DONE.md`.) If it only *partly*
     passes (some steps still owed), it **stays** with the passed parts noted and the remainder вҸі.
   - **Recurring item** (`рҹҢҗ` endpoint-liveness / any `Cadence: every N days`): it **stays here** вҖ”
     don't archive it. Just record the run: flip the status, set `Last checked`, bump `Next check` by
     the `Cadence`. These are meant to be re-run forever.
   - A **вқҢ** stays вқҢ (with the date + what broke) until it's re-fixed and re-run вҖ” never archive a fail.
4. **Only if no browser is reachable:** leave the item logged here and move on вҖ” don't block on
   Michael. Do **not** mark anything вң… from reading the code вҖ” confirming-in-the-running-app is the
   entire point of this file.
5. **Endpoint-liveness items (tagged рҹҢҗ) are the exception to "needs a browser"** вҖ” a `curl`/REST
   probe, runnable without a browser. Run those when due (and per rule 3 they stay, they don't archive).

`CLAUDE.md` points every session here, so this list is consulted automatically.

---

- **Verified here (sandbox, logged-out):** the new self-contained headless harness `ui-audit/verify-b644-fresh-null.mjs` (serves the embed's four CDN deps from local copies via request interception вҖ” the old "sandbox can't boot the embed" blocker is stale) reproduced the exact owner error + stack pre-fix on the identical Start blank вҶ’ Schedule flow, and PASSES post-fix (embed renders, zero null-`projects` console/page errors). Root cause pinned by the captured stack: the shellвҶ’iframe `planar:nav-*` bridge queued `setData(d => вҖҰ)` updaters before the async `hs-v1` load resolved, and React ran them with `d === null` inside the next `useState` mount. What's left is the live cold-network race the sandbox can't time-shift вҖ” the deterministic half is proven.

New `lib/deedAlign.js` solves the **rigid** rotation+translation to overlay the deed on the held parcel (scale locked вҖ” deed dimensions preserved; holes move as one group); a one-click **"Align to parcel"** banner + panel button + a manual RotateВ° stepper apply it and report the rotation + fit residual honestly.

So the tool behaves correctly (rotates to best fit, honestly flags "loose вҖ” verify") but the real misalignment is **partly rotation, partly that the loaded GIS outline isn't the same polygon as the deed** (parent/adjacent tract, or the wrong lot selected). **Separately:** the **"94.91 acres"** plot is a **0.38 ac / 119 ft-wide sliver** вҖ” a bad metes-and-bounds *parse* of that description (see B626), not an alignment problem.

  3. **B616 finish lock:** type a **Finish** date on a task вҶ’ a **padlock icon** appears on the Finish cell (identical to the Start pin). Slip an upstream predecessor so the chain would push past that locked finish вҶ’ the finish **holds** (doesn't move) and a **loud red banner** + a red вҡ  on the row appear ("N task can't meet its locked finish date"). Click the padlock вҶ’ the finish **unlocks** and flows from start + duration again.
  4. **B624 weekend guard:** type a **Saturday or Sunday** (or a known holiday) into a task's **Start** or **Finish** cell вҶ’ confirm it **jumps forward to the next working day** and a **toast** says it moved because you picked a weekend/holiday. A normal weekday entry is accepted with no toast.

### V194 вҖ” B613 + B634 (the fix; commit/PR + in-code/test labels keep the provisional B630): a Fort Bend parcel click/search must NOT flash the "statewide backup" notice when FBCAD is healthy вқҢ FAIL found live 2026-07-03 (false notice on EVERY FB click) вҶ’ рҹ”§ root-caused + fix shipped (B630 label + B643 eager-race) вҶ’ вҸі live re-verify owed (sandbox Chromium egress resets all GIS hosts, so the click-through can't run here)
- **Added** 2026-07-02 В· **Cadence** once (fix acceptance) В· **Last checked** 2026-07-03 (Cowork, signed in on planyr.io вҖ” **FAILED**, see below; then B630 fix: lint 0 В· **2281 tests green** incl. 6 new `isStatewideBackup` cases В· build green) В· **Next check** вҖ” on planyr.io, in a real browser, confirm the false notice is GONE (no sign-in needed вҖ” the parcel layer is public/anonymous).
- **вқҢ What the live run found (Cowork, 2026-07-03):** on the live signed-in map, **3 independent Fort Bend clicks all showed the amber "Statewide backup вҖ” Fort Bend county's server is unavailable; shown from TxGIO" notice** вҖ” including a plain residential rooftop. Decisive evidence it was a code bug, not FBCAD being down: a direct in-page `fetch()` of the FBCAD Esri endpoint for the exact clicked point returned **HTTP 200, featureCount = 1** with the full FBCAD schema, and the network tab showed **the app itself calling that same FBCAD URL and getting 200 on every click** вҖ” so FBCAD's primary was up and answering, yet the app labeled it unavailable.
- **рҹ”§ Root cause (B630) вҖ” NOT the circuit breaker (the live report's hypothesis was close but off).** The breaker correctly ignores "200 + 0 features" (B245), and it was CLOSED (FBCAD was being queried, per the 200s). The real culprit: the click path (`identifyParcelEager`) races the county CAD and the statewide TxGIO layer **in parallel and takes the first to answer** вҖ” and FBCAD's Esri layer is a hair slower than TxGIO's identify, so **TxGIO kept WINNING THE RACE**. The old `viaBackup = STATEWIDE_KEYS.includes(hit.county) && realPrimaries.length > 0` then read "the statewide source answered" as "the county server is down" вҖ” a false alarm on every healthy click.
- **вң… Fix shipped (B630, this branch):** new pure `isStatewideBackup()` in `lib/sourceHealth.js` вҖ” a statewide answer is flagged a "backup" **only when the county's own CAD was genuinely unavailable this click** (its breaker was open вҶ’ it was dropped from the query), never when a healthy CAD was queried but merely lost the parallel race. Wired into both the map-click (`handleClick`) and the search-select (`selectParcelAt`) paths in `MapFinder.jsx`. Proven here: lint 0 В· full suite **2281 green** (incl. 6 new B630 cases: race-lost вҮ’ no notice, breaker-open вҮ’ real backup, statewide-only area, border straddle) В· build green.
- **рҹ”§ Follow-on fix (B643, this branch) вҖ” the eager RACE itself, so FBCAD's OWN data shows (V194 step 3):** B630 made the *notice* honest, but TxGIO still won the parallel race, so a Fort Bend click could select TxGIO's coarser copy (missing FBCAD's appraisal values). B643 tags identify candidates with `statewide` and has `identifyParcelEager` (`lib/arcgis.js`) **prefer a healthy real CAD** вҖ” a real-CAD hit resolves immediately; a statewide hit waits a bounded ~1.2s `BACKUP_GRACE_MS` for an in-flight CAD before being accepted вҖ” so a healthy FBCAD wins the race and its own parcel/appraisal data shows, while a genuinely-hung CAD still can't stall the click past the grace (the B244 eager guarantee holds). With the CAD winning, `hit.county` is the CAD (not statewide), so `isStatewideBackup` is doubly false. Proven here: lint 0 В· **2429 tests green** (post `origin/main` merge; incl. my 3 new eager-preference/grace cases in `test/arcgis.test.js`) В· build green. If a healthy FBCAD still loses the race in the field, the grace is a one-line tune.
- **вҸі Why the live re-verify still pends (not auth вҖ” a sandbox egress limit):** this sandbox's Chromium **resets every external GIS host** (`services2.arcgis.com`, `feature.geographic.texas.gov` вҶ’ `net::ERR_CONNECTION_RESET`; curl through the agent proxy reaches them fine, so it's a browser-egress gap, not the code). `gis-verify/fbcad-hosted-primary-verify.mjs` is ready to run the moment a browser can reach the host.
- **вҸі Steps on planyr.io (any teammate with an unrestricted browser вҖ” NOT Michael's job):**
  1. Open the Site Planner over **Fort Bend County** (Sugar Land / Katy / Richmond area). Click **Select parcels**, zoom to ~street level вҶ’ confirm parcel **outlines paint** promptly.
  2. **Click several Fort Bend lots** (incl. a residential rooftop) вҶ’ each selects, and the on-canvas amber **"statewide backupвҖҰ"** notice does **NOT** appear (this is the B630 regression вҖ” it must be gone now that FBCAD answering, or merely losing the race, no longer trips the "unavailable" flag).
  3. Confirm the selected lot's **Appraisal data** shows owner, situs, values (Land/Improvement/Total), acreage, legal, land use.
  4. In the planner's **Add parcel вҶ’ Identify from county GIS**, search a Fort Bend **account (R-number / QuickRef ID)** and a **site address** вҶ’ both return the right lot with no false backup notice.
  5. Sanity: Harris and Chambers parcels still work unchanged; and if FBCAD is ever *genuinely* down (force it / its breaker opens), a click SHOULD still fall back to TxGIO **with** the honest backup notice.

### V169 вҖ” B555: planner two-finger pinch rewritten on native touch events вң… headless 3/3 here; вҸі real iOS Safari pinch owed
- **What changed (2026-06-28, branch `claude/mobile-safari-pinch-menu-3gon8x`).** The Site Planner canvas drove its two-finger pinch off **pointer** events; iOS Safari handles multi-touch pointer events unreliably (it commonly fires a spurious `pointercancel` on the first finger when a second lands вҖ” killing the pinch mid-gesture and letting a one-finger pan fight it вҶ’ the owner's "super buggy" report). Rewrote pinch on **native touch** events (`onTouchStart/Move/End`), which carry all active touches in `e.touches` every frame; updates are throttled to one per animation frame; the pre-pinch one-finger pan is reverted so the gesture can't jump in; pointer pan/draw/vertex handlers bail while вүҘ2 fingers are down. `touch-action: none` already suppresses the browser default, so the passive touch handlers need no preventDefault.
- **вң… Verified here (headless, CDP multi-touch, 390Г—844).** `ui-audit/verify-planner-pinch.mjs` 3/3: pinch-out zooms in (0.25вҶ’1.88 px/ft), pinch-in within the same gesture zooms back out (1.88вҶ’0.25), and a second pinch still works (canvas not left stuck). lint 0 В· 1782 tests В· build green.
- **вҸі Why pending (the actual iOS flakiness only reproduces on a real iPhone/iPad вҖ” headless Chromium's pointer multi-touch is well-behaved, so it can't exhibit the bug being fixed).** On a real device in the planner: pinch to zoom in/out repeatedly and confirm it's smooth, never jumps, never sticks in a pan, and that one-finger pan + drawing still work between pinches.
- Cadence: once after ship.

### V158 вҖ” B501/B502/B503: Schedule delete-recompute + InlineDate year-keep + MasterView date guard вң… unit + esbuild-parse here; вҸі three running-app click-throughs owed
- **What changed (2026-06-27, branch `claude/app-loops-debug-hukhfz`).** Three Schedule-module fixes from the bug-hunt: **B501** вҖ” deleting a task now recomputes parent roll-ups/cascade (`deleteTask`/`deleteTasks` wrap the filtered list with `recomputeAfterStructureChange`), so a parent summary bar no longer shows a stale span after a child is deleted; **B502** вҖ” `InlineDate` keeps the year (seeds with `toShortDate`), so editing a non-current-year date no longer silently rewrites it to this year; **B503** вҖ” `MasterView.fmtDate` guards a non-ISO value so the dashboard never prints `NaN/NaN/yy`.

### V143 вҖ” Signed-in resume-into-planner after reload (B478 вҖ” the V13/V28 HIGH-PRIORITY fix) вҸі signed-in confirm owed; logged-out no-regression вң…
- **Added** 2026-06-25 В· **Cadence** once (HIGH-PRIORITY bug-fix acceptance) В· **Last checked** вҖ” В· **Next check** the signed-in steps below, on the branch preview / planyr.io after deploy. **Claude cohort's job, never Michael's.**
- **What changed (B478).** Signed-in, a deep link / refresh into a project (`#/project/<id>/site`) used to **bounce to the finder** (route stripped to `#/`) because the cloud sites aren't loaded at the first synchronous render, so a transient null active-project got written over the route AND nulled the `currentSite` pointer before `pullCloud` finished. A `bootResolved` gate (pure `lib/bootResume.js`) now holds the URL sync + the dangling-pointer cleanup until the first auth + pull settles; one shared `pickResumeTarget` picks the plan.
- **вң… Already proven without sign-in:** lint 0 В· **1585 tests (+11 `bootResume.test.js`)** В· build green; logged-out headless **8/8** (`ui-audit/verify-resume-into-planner.mjs` вҖ” deep-link + reload stays in the planner, route intact, `currentSite` preserved, 0 page errors) + `verify-new-site-save.mjs` **10/10** (no regression on the new-site boot/save/reload path). The signed-in async-pull gap (the literal repro) **can't be driven in the sandbox** (no Supabase configured вҶ’ no async gap; `bootResolved` starts true), so the end-to-end signed-in resume is the one owed check.
- **Steps (signed in, on planyr.io / the branch preview):**
  1. Sign in вҶ’ open **8 South** (or any cloud site) вҶ’ the planner loads (URL `#/project/<id>/site`).
  2. **Reload** (soft F5 AND hard Ctrl+Shift+R). **Expect:** you **resume straight into that project's planner** вҖ” NOT bounced to the finder; the URL **stays** `#/project/<id>/site` (not stripped to `#/`); the breadcrumb names the project (not "Select a project"); the exact open plan (not just the newest) is shown.
  3. **Cold deep link:** paste `https://planyr.io/#/project/<id>/site` into a fresh tab (signed in). **Expect:** it opens that project's planner directly, no finder bounce.
  4. **Tab-refocus trigger:** switch away ~2вҖ“3 min, return. **Expect:** still in the planner, no bounce (the same-user re-emit is skipped; `bootResolved` is already true post-boot).
- **If it fails (still bounces to `#/`):** capture the URL at boot + the console; this is the HIGH-PRIORITY resume class вҖ” flag it. (No data-loss risk either way вҖ” durability is independently вң….)

### V135 вҖ” B460: no spurious "changed in another session" conflict on a benign re-open вң… 3 unit tests (mergePulledSites content-diff toPush) + lint 0 + 1506 tests + build green; вҸі one signed-in two-tab benign-reopen check (Cowork)

Now the boot re-push fires only when the merge actually changed content (add/move/tombstoned-delete), not on a mere timestamp bump. (`storage.js` `contentSig` + `toPush`.)

### V134 вҖ” B459: cloud-save content guard (never silently overwrite a fuller row with a thin one) вң… 9 unit tests (`wouldThinClobber`) + lint 0 + 1504 tests + build green; вҸі one signed-in stale-tab clobber repro (Cowork, Phase B)
- **What changed.** The cloud save's compare-and-swap checks only the version NUMBER, not content вҖ” so a stale/thin tab at a matching version could overwrite a fuller cloud row (the 8 South 5-building loss). Now the save remembers the content baseline it last synced and BLOCKS a push that would drop вүҘ2 items the cloud still has with no delete-tombstone, surfacing the B455 loud+blocking conflict instead of clobbering (the cloud stays intact вҶ’ reload union-merges it back). (`cloudSync.js` `wouldThinClobber` + `siteContent`/`siteTombs`.)
- **Verified (sandbox).** Pure decision unit-tested deterministically (`test/cloudThinGuard.test.js`, 9 cases): the 5-building clobber blocks; a single undo passes; a tombstoned bulk delete passes; partial-tombstone and boundary (lost-2 vs lost-1) cases; cross-collection counting.

### V133 вҖ” B458: immediate per-edit local-mirror write (the real data-loss fix) вң… logged-out headless 6/6 (`ui-audit/verify-immediate-mirror.mjs`) + 3 unit tests + lint 0 + 1495 tests + build green; вҸі one signed-in survive-a-reload cloud round-trip (Cowork, Phase B)
- **What changed.** The Site Planner autosave used to debounce BOTH the on-device localStorage mirror AND the version-history snapshot by 400 ms, so a reload within that window lost the edit from cloud, mirror, AND history at once (the structural cause of the 8 South / Plan 1 building-loss, per Cowork's live Phase-A diagnosis). Now the device mirror is written **immediately** on every edit (history on вҶ’ the rollback snapshot is reload-safe too); only the cloud push stays debounced. (`SitePlanner.jsx` autosave split; `storage.js` `saveSite({ skipHistory })`.)
- **Verified (sandbox, logged-out).** `verify-immediate-mirror.mjs` 6/6: an edit is in the device mirror at **150 ms** вҖ” before the 400 ms debounce (would be ABSENT under the old code) вҖ” the history snapshot is present at 150 ms too, and the edit **survives an immediate reload**. 3 new `storage.test.js` cases assert `skipHistory` suppresses the snapshot but persists content, the default still snapshots, and the immediate-then-settle shape backs up the prior version exactly once.
- **Why вҸі (Cowork, signed-in вҖ” NOT markable from the sandbox).** **Survive-a-reload with a real cloud row:** sign in, add buildings, reload immediately mid-edit вҶ’ after reload (and on a second device) all buildings are present, because boot's union-merge now always has the fuller local copy to restore + re-push. The logged-out sandbox proves the local-mirror timing; the cloud round-trip needs auth. Part of Phase B (run after this deploys). Cadence: once after ship.

### V122 вҖ” Live PK is single-column `id`; docs corrected + degrade-branch upserts repointed (B280 follow-up) вң… cloud-save round-trip VERIFIED LIVE (Cowork 2026-06-25); вҸі only the version-LESS-DB fallback branch stays dormant/untested (latent-path hardening)
- **вң… 2026-06-25 (Cowork, signed-in on planyr.io):** an edit (drew + deleted a markup in a Review) **autosaved and the header read "Cloud sync: Synced"** вҖ” the primary `casUpsert` (keyed on `id`) round-trip works live. The version-LESS-DB id-first fallback stays dormant on production (the `version` column exists there), so that branch is still untested вҖ” low-priority latent-path hardening, not a user-facing gap.
- **What changed.** A Cowork session with live-DB access confirmed (via `pg_constraint`) that
  `public.sites` AND `public.doc_reviews` have **`PRIMARY KEY (id)`** on planyr-production вҖ” NOT the
  `(user_id, id)` the docs claimed. That drift had already been migrated in by `db/team_sharing.sql`
  (PK `(user_id,id)вҶ’(id)` so one row per project survives a teammate edit); `user_id` stays the
  owner column + RLS predicate. Fixed three things: (1) the two `CLAUDE.md` "Table schema" blocks
  now say `primary key (id)` with a note; (2) the **degrade-branch** plain-upserts in `cloudSync.js`
  (`sites`) and `reviewStore.js` (`doc_reviews`) were keyed on `onConflict:"user_id,id"` alone вҖ”
  which 42P10s on the live single-column PK вҖ” now they try `"id"` first and fall back to
  `"user_id,id"` only for a genuinely pre-migration DB, mirroring `upsertFileFacts`' existing pattern;
  (3) the B280 seed (`e2e/seed/seed.sql`) was already made constraint-independent.
- **Why вҸі.** The degrade branch only fires when the `version` column is absent; on production the
  column exists, so the fixed path is dormant there (the primary `casUpsert` already keys on `id`).
  The seed itself is вң… confirmed live. The owed check is one signed-in save against a DB lacking the
  `version` column, to watch the new id-first fallback succeed вҖ” low priority (latent-path hardening).
- **Steps / Expect.** Sign in вҶ’ edit a site вҶ’ Save shows "Saved" (cloud write ok). On a version-less
  DB the network call upserts with `onConflict=id` and does not 42P10. Cadence: once. Last checked: вҖ”.
- **2026-07-01 (Cowork):** Re-verified independently via the Supabase MCP connector (read-only) against `planyr_production` (`lyeqzkuiwngunutlkkmi`): (A) the B280 fixture row is present вҖ” the `sites`вӢҲ`auth.users` join on `e2e@planyr.test` / `id='e2e-fixture-site'` returns **exactly one row** (name "E2E Fixture вҖ” Markup Harness", county Harris, user_id `a96e544f-8537-45cf-81a2-007965fbc04c`); (B) `pg_constraint` confirms **both PKs are single-column** вҖ” `sites_pkey = PRIMARY KEY (id)`, `doc_reviews_pkey = PRIMARY KEY (id)`. This corroborates the 2026-06-23 SQL-editor check via a second access path. Also confirmed the `CLAUDE.md` PK-block fix is live in `main`. **Still вҸі (unchanged):** the low-priority version-less-DB id-first fallback round-trip (dormant on prod, which has the `version` column).

  - County `https://services.arcgis.com/KTcxiTD9dsQw4r7Z/arcgis/rest/services/Texas_County_Boundaries/FeatureServer/0?f=json`
  - City `https://feature.geographic.texas.gov/arcgis/rest/services/City_Boundaries/Texas_City_Boundaries/MapServer/0?f=json`

### V9 вҖ” Attach & mark up a drawing on a parcel (B67) вң… attach + sheet-picker + cloud persistence / вҸі markup-draw not driver-testable
- **Added** 2026-06-16 В· **Cadence** once (feature acceptance) В· **Last checked** 2026-06-20 вң… (Cowork + owner did the OS file-pick) В· **Next check** вҖ”
- **вң… Mostly VERIFIED 2026-06-20 (Cowork signed-in + owner did the OS file-pick).** Selected Parcel 1 вҶ’ Parcel panel вҶ’ **пјӢ Attach a drawing** вҶ’ picked a 2-page PDF: the **"Pick a sheet" dialog listed both pages**; chose p.1 and the sheet **rasterized as an immutable backdrop named "<file> вҖ” p.1"** (saved to `parcelDrawings[]` with a cloud `storageKey`). After a **full reload + reopen-from-finder** the drawing **reloaded from the cloud and the backdrop re-rasterized** in the editor (Pen / Line / Box / Text / Measure / Scale toolbar all present). So attach вҶ’ multi-page sheet-pick вҶ’ rasterized backdrop вҶ’ save-with-parcel вҶ’ cross-reload persistence are confirmed live, signed-in.
- **вҸі Not directly driven:** drawing markups on the sheet + their persistence вҖ” the markup editor's draw interactions don't register through the browser-automation layer (drags read as clicks; text placement doesn't focus), the same input limit hit on the planner canvas (not an app bug). Markup persistence rides the same `markups[]` cloud path already proven for the easement (V39), so it's covered by analogy; a human drawing one markup + reload would fully close it.
- **NB (tooling):** the parcel-drawing file `<input>` can't be filled programmatically (synthetic upload doesn't stick; the native file dialog is suppressed under automation), so this attach needs a real OS file-pick by a human вҖ” relevant for future verification runs.
- **Steps:** Open a site, select a **parcel** вҶ’ Parcel panel вҶ’ **"пјӢ Attach a drawing (PDF / JPG)"**
  вҶ’ pick a real **multi-page** engineering PDF (then also a JPEG). For the multi-page PDF a
  **"Pick a sheet"** dialog should list every page вҖ” choose one. Draw with **Pen / Line / Box /
  Text**, recolour, **Select** + **Delete**, **zoom (wheel) + pan (drag in Select)**, click
  **Done**, reopen the drawing, then **reload the page**.
- **Richer markup (increment 2c) вҖ” also verify:** in **Select**, **drag an existing markup** to
  reposition it (cursor shows move); **double-click a Text** markup to edit it. Click **Scale**,
  draw a line along a known dimension, enter its length in feet вҶ’ then **Measure**: draw lines and
  confirm they label the **real length in feet** (teal chip); the scale + markups persist on reload.
- **Expect:** the **chosen** sheet rasterizes as an **immutable backdrop** (named "<file> вҖ” p.N");
  markups stay **locked to the drawing** through zoom/pan (stored pixel-relative); multiple
  drawings list under the parcel; markups **persist** across reopen + reload (signed in, same
  device). `ui-audit/screens/parcel-drawing.png` shows the modal headless (an SVG stand-in, not a
  real PDF) вҖ” this step confirms it with a real file, including the page-picker.
- **Cross-device (increment 2b, landed 2026-06-16) вҖ” please test:** signed in, attach a drawing on
  device A; on **device B** (or after clearing local cache) open the same site + drawing вҶ’ the
  backdrop should **rebuild from cloud Storage** ("Loading the drawing from the cloudвҖҰ", then it
  appears with its markups). The source file is uploaded to the private `doc-review-files` bucket at
  `<uid>/parcel-drawings/<siteId>/<drawingId>.<ext>`; on reopen without a local raster it re-fetches +
  re-rasterizes the stored sheet. Deleting a drawing removes its stored object. **Fallback:** logged
  out / >50 MB / upload error вҶ’ keeps the local raster + the old "re-attach" placeholder cross-device
  (markups always persist), so nothing regresses.
- **Increment 2a (multi-page sheet picker) also landed** вҖ” verify the "Pick a sheet" dialog lists all
  pages and attaches the chosen one.

### V10 вҖ” Snap defaults OFF; toggle + Alt hold-to-suppress (B114) вң… default-OFF confirmed live (Cowork 2026-06-25); вҸі the S-toggle + Alt-hold + persistence still owed

NOT separately exercised: the S-key / pill toggle to "Snap 10вҖІ", the Alt-hold-to-suppress for one drag, and the on/off persistence across sites/reload вҖ” those stay вҸі below.

- **Steps:** (0) Open **any** site вҖ” incl. an existing one made before this change вҖ” and confirm the
  toolbar pill reads **`Snap off`** (grey dot) and dragging a road up against trailer parking does
  **not** stick to its edge (it lands where you drop it). (1) Press **S** (cursor on the canvas, not
  in a text field) вҶ’ pill flips to **`Snap 10вҖІ`** (green dot); now the road flush-snaps to the edge.
  (2) **Hold Alt** and drag it to a deliberate ~15-ft gap and drop вҖ” with snap on, Alt still places
  it freely for that one move; release Alt and snapping is back. (3) Click the toolbar **Snap** pill вҖ”
  same toggle as S. (4) Turn snap on, **switch to another site / reload the page** вҶ’ snap stays **on**
  (the choice persists); turn it off вҶ’ stays off. (5) With snap on, resize a box / rotate it (grid /
  15В° steps) vs. Alt-held (smooth/free).
- **Expect:** Snap starts **OFF for every site** (free movement is the default, even on old sites that
  had snap baked in). The **S** key, the pill, and the Setup checkbox all toggle one **global**
  preference that persists across sites/reloads. Alt suppresses snapping for just that one drag and
  re-enables on release; "off" fully disables grid snap, neighbour flush-snap, resize-to-grid and
  rotate-to-15В°. **Shift-drag still bonds to a neighbour** (the green +) regardless of the toggle.
- **If it fails:** none critical (no data risk) вҖ” log вқҢ here with what looked wrong.

### V11 вҖ” Phone layout (B113) + "Cloud off" affordance (B111) + header scroll-not-clip (B485) вҸі physical-device touch/rotation owed; headless вң…
- **вң… FIX SHIPPED 2026-06-27 (B485, PR #376; renumbered from a provisional B481 a concurrent `main` took) вҖ” the shared header now scrolls sideways instead of clipping.** Driving this item under REAL mobile emulation (iPhone-13, which the Cowork `resize_window` tool couldn't produce) exposed a genuine defect the prior 390Г—844 screenshots missed: the two-row `AppHeader` overran the phone width and **clipped its controls** (the project/plan switcher, the save/settings/auth badges, and the whole Row-2 toolbar вҖ” only "вҖҰcels" + "File в–ҫ" survived), the opposite of this test's own spec ("scroll sideways, not wrap"). The B113 phone work had fixed the planner *body* but never the shared header. Fixed in `AppHeader.jsx` via `useNarrow()` (matchMedia `max-width:760px`): each header row now `overflow-x:auto` + zones at natural width (no clip), the brand drops to the mark on phone, Schedule's center-slot Row-2 switches wrapвҶ’scroll; all `narrow ?`-gated so **desktop is byte-identical**. Verified: lint 0 В· full test suite green В· build green В· new headless **`ui-audit/verify-phone-layout.mjs`** (real iPhone-13 emulation) **10/10, stable 3Г—**, with a regression guard that FAILS pre-fix (clip, `maxRowOverflow=0`) and PASSES post-fix (scroll, `360px`); phone Site/Review/Schedule + desktop shots all clean. Re-verified after merging the latest `main`.
- **вҸі Why still вҸі (physical device only):** the headless run proves the layout/scroll on an emulated phone; **real-finger touch + rotation to landscape and back** still want an actual handheld (the sandbox has no touch device and can't rotate). Everything below is otherwise headless-confirmed.
- **Steps (B113, on a phone or a ~390px-wide window):** open a site in the planner. The canvas
  should fill the width (not a sliver). Tap the orange **"вңҺ Tools"** button (bottom-right) вҶ’ the tool
  palette **slides in from the right**; pick a tool вҶ’ it **auto-closes** so you can draw; tap the dim
  backdrop to dismiss it. Tap a left-rail button (Yield/Parcel/вҖҰ) вҶ’ its panel **overlays** the canvas;
  tap the same button to close. Rotate to landscape and back. The top header should **scroll
  sideways**, not wrap onto two lines.
- **Expect:** at desktop width everything is exactly as before (the mobile styles are width-gated).
- **Steps (B111):** load a build with **no Supabase env** (cloud unconfigured). The top-right account
  corner should show a muted **"вҠҳ Cloud off"** pill (not empty); click it вҶ’ a popover explains work is
  saved on this device only. (A configured build still shows the normal Sign in / account button.)

### V12 вҖ” Site Planner measurement tools: Length / Polylength / Area (B116) вң… mode menu confirmed live (Cowork 2026-06-25); вҸі the draw round-trip + uncalibrated-warning still owed
- **вң… 2026-06-25 (Cowork, signed-in in 8 South's planner):** the **Measure** tool dropdown offers **Length / Polylength / Area** (+ Count). NOT driven: actually drawing each mode + the labels, and the amber "вҡ  Underlay isn't calibrated" path вҖ” those stay вҸі below.
- **Added** 2026-06-16 В· **Cadence** once (feature acceptance) В· **Last checked** 2026-06-25 (mode menu вң…) В· **Next check** the draw round-trip below
- **Steps:** Open a site in the Site Planner. Right rail вҶ’ **Measure** (the `в–ҫ` opens the mode menu:
  **Length / Polylength / Area**). (1) **Length:** click two points вҶ’ expect a teal line labeled the
  real distance in feet (e.g. `462вҖІ`). (2) **Polylength:** click several points along a path, then
  **double-click or Enter** to finish вҶ’ expect the running path length in feet. (3) **Area:** click
  points around a region, close by clicking the first dot (or double-click) вҶ’ expect a filled polygon
  labeled **`<sf> sf В· <ac> ac В· <perim>вҖІ perim`** (e.g. `12,300 sf В· 0.28 ac В· 462вҖІ perim`). Then
  with **Select**, click a measurement to select it and use the **Г—** to delete it. Press **Esc**
  mid-draw вҶ’ the in-progress measurement cancels.
- **Calibration path:** drop an **aerial/screenshot** underlay but do **not** calibrate it вҶ’ with the
  Measure tool active, expect the **"вҡ  Underlay isn't calibrated вҖ” distances may be wrong"** banner and
  measurement labels rendered in **amber with a вҡ **. Calibrate the underlay (Aerial в–ҫ вҶ’ Calibrate) вҶ’
  labels return to normal (teal) and read true feet.
- **Expect:** all three modes draw, label, select, and delete; labels persist across reopen + reload
  (signed in); the amber/вҡ  uncalibrated warning behaves as above. This shipped code-verified +
  build-green (B116 was already implemented in `SitePlanner.jsx`; only the mode names were aligned to
  Length/Polylength/Area) вҖ” this step confirms it in the running app.
- **If it fails:** not critical (no data risk) вҖ” log вқҢ here with what looked wrong.

### V13 вҖ” вҳ… Persistence: saved work must never disappear (B124 / B125) вҖ” durability вң… / resume-into-planner: вқҢ confirmed 2026-06-25 вҶ’ **FIX SHIPPED same session (B478)**, signed-in confirm owed вҖ” HIGH PRIORITY
- **Added** 2026-06-16 В· **Cadence** once (data-safety acceptance) + on-change В· **Last checked** 2026-06-25 (Cowork re-confirmed вқҢ; fix then shipped вҖ” see below) В· **Next check** the signed-in resume confirm (now **V143**)
- **вқҢ RE-CONFIRMED 2026-06-25 (Cowork, signed-in on planyr.io), then ROOT-CAUSE PINNED + FIXED the same session.** Cowork opened **8 South** (URL `#/project/smqiljx5fngg/site`, planner rendered), ran `location.reload()` вҶ’ at both ~2 s and ~7 s the app **bounced to the finder**, breadcrumb "Select a project", URL **stripped to `#/`**; a cold navigate straight to a project URL likewise bounced. Data durability is fine (8 South stays intact + reopenable) вҖ” it's purely the resume UX.
- **вң… FIX SHIPPED this session (B478, branch `claude/v13-resume-into-planner`).** ROOT CAUSE found in `SitePlannerApp.jsx`: on a **signed-in** deep link/refresh the user's cloud sites aren't in the local store at the first synchronous render (auth + `pullCloud` are async), so `activeSiteId` is momentarily null even though the route names a project. Two boot reactions then destroyed the resume **before** the pull could finish: (1) the active-projectвҶ’URL sync wrote that transient `null` over the route, **stripping `#/project/<id>/site` вҶ’ `#/`** (and bouncing to the finder); (2) the "tidy a dangling `currentSite`" cleanup **nulled the pointer** because the cloud site only *looked* absent. FIX: a `bootResolved` gate (pure `lib/bootResume.js`) holds BOTH reconciliations until the first auth + pull settles; the resume target is now one shared, unit-tested `pickResumeTarget`. Verified: lint 0 В· **1585 tests (+11 `bootResume.test.js`)** В· build green В· logged-out headless **8/8** (`ui-audit/verify-resume-into-planner.mjs` вҖ” deep-link + reload stays in the planner, route intact, pointer preserved) + `verify-new-site-save.mjs` **10/10** (no regression). **The signed-in async-gap repro can't run in the sandbox (no Supabase вҶ’ no gap), so the signed-in confirm is owed вҖ” tracked as V143 below.**
- **2026-06-20 (Cowork вҖ” real signed-in Chrome on planyr.io, cloud ON; deployed bundle SitePlannerApp-BuRTao7i.js, Supabase HTTP 200 each boot, no console errors):**
  - **вң… Data durability (the critical part):** drew 3 buildings on a signed-in throwaway site; "Synced вң“"; the site + every element survived **~6 reloads** and reopened intact from the finder. Work never disappeared on its own.
  - **вқҢ Resume-into-planner (step 2):** every reload вҖ” **soft (F5) AND hard (Ctrl+Shift+R)**, on a brand-new site AND an established/reopened site вҖ” lands on the **map/finder**, NOT the open planner. Confirmed at the storage layer: `currentSite:v1` holds the open site's id going *into* the reload, and boot **nulls it** and shows the finder; even force-setting `currentSite:v1` in localStorage then reloading still nulled it вҶ’ finder. No crash, no data loss вҖ” but it contradicts the written "resume straight into the planner, NOT bounced to the map" expectation. (Matches the prior "reload bounces NEW sites to finder" note, but now reproduces for established sites too.)
  - Steps 4 (DevTools offline) & 5 (signed-outвҶ’sign-in bridge) not run: the offline toggle isn't drivable via the browser tools, and re-sign-in requires a password Cowork won't enter. Worth a manual pass.
- **Why this matters:** this is the fix for the owner-reported data-loss scare вҖ” work vanishing on its
  own a couple minutes after a reload. Root cause: `pullCloud` rebuilt the local cache from the cloud
  list **alone** and silently dropped any not-yet-synced local site; the resume then couldn't find the
  open site and bounced to the map. Confirm in a real browser that saved work is now durable.
- **Steps (signed in, on planyr.io):**
  1. Sign in. Open or create a site, add a **building**; wait for the header badge to read **"Synced вң“"**.
  2. **Reload** вҶ’ you **resume straight into the planner** on that site (NOT bounced to the map) and the
     building is still there.
  3. **Switch to another browser tab for ~2вҖ“3 minutes, then return** (refocus the Planyr tab) вҶ’ the site
     + building must **still be there** and you are **not** bounced to the map. (This is the exact
     "disappears on its own" trigger вҖ” a background re-sign-in event firing the cloud re-pull.)
  4. **Forced not-yet-synced repro (DevTools):** Network tab вҶ’ **Offline**. Add another building вҶ’ a
     **loud red banner** ("your last change didn't reach the cloud вҖҰ **Retry now**") appears and the badge
     reads Offline/Unsaved. **Reload while still offline** вҶ’ the building is **still there** (not dropped).
     Go back **Online** вҶ’ it syncs (badge вҶ’ "Synced вң“") and the red banner clears.
  5. **On-device вҶ’ account bridge:** while **signed out**, create a site (saved on this device only).
     **Sign in** вҶ’ a blue banner "You have N site(s) saved on **this device** that aren't in your account
     yet" appears; click **"Bring them into my account"** вҶ’ the site joins the account list and the banner
     clears. The signed-out copy is **kept** (non-destructive).
- **Expect:** work **never disappears on its own**; reload resumes the open site; a failed cloud save is
  **loud** (red banner + Retry), never silent; the on-device import copies sites into the account without
  deleting the originals. No data is lost across reload, tab-refocus, offline, or sign-in/out.
- **If it fails:** this is the one **CRITICAL** class вҖ” if saved work still vanishes, flag it immediately
  (note the exact step + the browser console), don't just log-and-move-on.

### V18 вҖ” Auto-numbered building labels: "Building N" + renumber-on-delete (B122) вң…

  appends as the next number. A site with a **single** building still reads "Building 1".

  delete a *lower-numbered* building so this one renumbers. Confirm the attached pieces stay attached and
  nothing re-points вҖ” attachment binds to the hidden stable id, not the visible number, so a renumber
  must never detach or mis-link anything.

  (car parking, paving, roads, detention ponds, sidewalks) are unaffected; bump-out pieces don't get

  unchanged), leaving a contiguous {1, 2} with no gap. Screenshot eyeballed; the static 4-line stack
  (name / sf / dims) rendered correctly too. (Attached-piece identity on renumber wasn't separately driven,
  but identity is keyed on the stable `el.id`, which the delete leaves untouched.)

- **Added** 2026-06-16 В· **Cadence** once (feature acceptance) В· **Last checked** 2026-06-25 (not driven) В· **Next check** 2026-06-16 вҖ” best driven headless on a seeded building with bump-outs at varied ppf

  bump-outs)"** вҖ” not the old "+2 bump-outs" вҖ” and there is **no** parenthetical line on a building with no
  bump-outs. (2) **Zoom out:** the **dimensions** line drops first, then the **(incl. вҖҰ)** line, leaving

### V22 вҖ” Red edge-dimension callouts hide when zoomed out (B121 round 2a) в—‘ callouts render confirmed (Cowork 2026-06-25); вҸі the hide-on-zoom-out LOD still owed
- **в—‘ 2026-06-25 (Cowork, signed-in in 8 South's planner):** the red **edge-dimension callouts render** on the building edges at a zoomed-in view. The **hide-on-zoom-out** LOD behavior wasn't cleanly driven (the Site-Planner SVG canvas doesn't zoom on double-click; the +/вҖ“ zoom buttons were avoided to prevent renderer freezes under map+GIS load) вҖ” stays вҸі below. Best driven by a headless harness that sets ppf directly.
- **Added** 2026-06-16 В· **Cadence** once (feature acceptance) В· **Last checked** 2026-06-25 (render в—‘) В· **Next check** 2026-06-16
- **Steps:** Open a site with a building / road / paving element (these carry the red short-side dimension
  tick, e.g. "300вҖІ" / "24вҖІ"). (1) **Working zoom:** the red dimension callout shows exactly as before.
  (2) **Zoom out** until the site is small on screen вҶ’ the red dimension ticks **drop away** (rather than
  shrinking into illegible marks that overlap the centred name labels). (3) **Zoom back in** вҶ’ they return.
- **Expect:** at normal/zoomed-in working zoom nothing changed; only when zoomed out (past ~0.18 px/ft) do the
  red dimension callouts hide. The centred name/sf labels are governed separately (B121 increment 1) and are
  unaffected by this gate.
- **Known-not-yet (do NOT fail for these):** at working zoom the dimension callouts can still overlap a
  centred name on very crowded layouts (not yet in the collision pool), there's no explicit show/hide toggle,
  and no leader lines вҖ” all tracked under B121 increment 2.
- **If it fails:** not critical (no data risk) вҖ” log вқҢ here (e.g. dims vanishing at working zoom = threshold
  too high; still piling when zoomed out = gate not applied).

### V23 вҖ” Warning toasts: a newer message isn't blanked early by an older one (B56b) вҸі

  **encumbrance** plot, ~9 s banner) then immediately a shorter one (e.g. Calibrate with no underlay, or start a
  utility route with no building) вҖ” confirm the **second message stays up its own full time** and isn't wiped a
  few seconds early by the first one's timer. (2) Open a sticky instructional prompt right after a transient
  warning (utility routing вҶ’ **"Now click the building to serve."**) вҖ” it should **persist until you act**, not
  auto-clear from the prior timer. (3) Start a ditch **cross-section**, then click again to begin a second while
  the first is still sampling вҖ” the second click is ignored (no double run / flicker).
- **Expect:** the visible warning always reflects the latest message for its own duration; sticky prompts persist
  until the next action; no cross-section double-run.
- **If it fails:** not critical (cosmetic/UX, no data risk) вҖ” log вқҢ here with what looked wrong.

### V24 вҖ” "Print overlay" toggle includes the site-plan overlay in the print/export, exactly as shown (B131) вҸі (Cowork 2026-06-25: not driven вҖ” needs an overlay dropped + the print/export dialog driven)

  position, scale, rotation and opacity** as on screen, **above** the aerial, with **no** selection handles or

  honored both ways (it used to silently vanish whenever an underlay existed). (4) Export menu вҶ’ **Export PNG** вҶ’
  the visible overlay is included in the image.

  checked = WYSIWYG overlay in the output; unchecked = no overlay; editor chrome (handles, the "re-add me"
  placeholder) never prints; PNG export includes the visible overlay.

### V25 вҖ” Detention pond expansion: lock-as-existing baseline + storage gained (B132) вҡ пёҸ SUPERSEDED by V30 / B139
- вҡ пёҸ **Superseded 2026-06-17 by V30 / B139.** The "Lock as existing pond" button this verified was replaced by the **"Expand this pond"** mode (B139) вҖ” that exact flow no longer exists. The detention math + dashed ghost it checked live on and were re-verified under V30. No action; kept for history.
- **Added** 2026-06-17 В· **Cadence** once (feature acceptance) В· **Last checked** вҖ” В· **Next check** 2026-06-17
- **Steps:** Open a site, draw a **Detention Pond** (rectangle or click-points irregular). Select it вҶ’ the right
  panel's **Detention storage** section now ends with a **"Lock as existing pond"** button. (1) Click it вҶ’ a toast
  confirms the lock and a faint **dashed ghost** of the current outline appears under the pond. (2) Drag a corner /
  edit a vertex to **enlarge** the footprint (and/or raise **Total depth**) вҶ’ an **"Expansion vs. existing"** box
  shows **Existing storage**, **Proposed storage**, and a green **"Storage gained +X.XX ac-ft"** (plus cf) that
  updates live as you drag. (3) **Shrink** the pond below the baseline вҶ’ the line flips to red **"Storage lost"**.
  (4) **Clear** вҶ’ ghost and the comparison box disappear; depth/freeboard/slope are retained. (5) Save, reload the
  site вҶ’ the locked baseline (ghost + numbers) persists. (6) **Rotate** the pond before locking, then enlarge вҶ’ the
  ghost stays aligned to the real (rotated) original outline, not offset.
- **Expect:** the gain equals proposed вҲ’ existing computed with the SAME depth/slope method (so it's apples-to-
  apples); ghost lands exactly on the original outline for both rectangle and irregular ponds, rotated or not;
  numbers and ghost survive reload; "screening only вҖ” confirm with your civil engineer" caveat shown.
- **If it fails:** not critical (screening estimate, no data-loss risk) вҖ” log вқҢ here with what looked wrong (ghost
  offset/rotated, gain number not updating, baseline lost on reload).

### V28 вҖ” вҳ… Boot fix: no stale-plan flash on reload; signed-in resume shows the latest (B134) вҖ” was BLOCKED on V13; resume FIX SHIPPED 2026-06-25 (B478) вҶ’ now reachable, signed-in confirm owed вҖ” HIGH PRIORITY, SIGNED-IN ONLY
- **UNBLOCKED 2026-06-25.** This test was unreachable because reload never resumed into the planner (it bounced to the finder), so there was no plan paint to flash. That **resume-into-planner bug is now FIXED this session (B478 вҖ” the `bootResolved` gate; see V13/V143).** Once the fix is confirmed signed-in (V143), re-run this flash check on the same reload: it should resume straight into the latest plan with no older/thinner copy flashing first. Until then it stays owed (the sandbox has no Supabase, so the signed-in resume can't be driven here).
- **вқҢ / can't-confirm 2026-06-20 (Cowork вҖ” real signed-in Chrome on planyr.io, cloud ON; deployed bundle SitePlannerApp-BuRTao7i.js, Supabase HTTP 200, no console errors).** The premise of this test вҖ” a signed-in reload that *resumes into the planner* вҖ” **doesn't happen**: every reload (soft + hard) lands on the **finder**, and `currentSite:v1` is nulled on boot even when force-set (see V13). So the "no stale/thin plan flash on resume" can't be exercised вҖ” there's no resume to flash. Data is intact and reopenable. This needs the underlying resume-into-planner behavior fixed first (see V13/V28 cross-ref) before the flash question is even reachable.
- **Added** 2026-06-17 В· **Cadence** once (data-display acceptance) + on-change В· **Last checked** вҖ” В· **Next check** 2026-06-17
- **Why a signed-in coworker must run this вҖ” the one thing this session could NOT self-verify.** The fix lives entirely on the **signed-in boot path**: `SitePlannerApp` bumps a `loadEpoch` after `applyUser`'s `pullCloud`, folded into the planner's `key`, so the keyed planner re-reads the freshly-merged cloud copy instead of lingering on the stale pre-auth one. Per the testing policy at the top of this file, the sandbox egress proxy **CORS-blocks the Supabase auth handshake**, so the in-session headless run is **logged-out only** вҖ” it confirmed the build (lint 0 В· 197 tests В· build green) and that logged-out behavior is byte-identical (the fix is gated to the signed-in branch; `loadEpoch` stays 0), but the actual signed-in resume can't be exercised here.
- **Already confirmed live (no browser):** shipped via **PR #103** вҶ’ `main` and **deployed** вҖ” planyr.io serves `index-DVWCJQ1q.js` / `SitePlannerApp-BUX0faXJ.js`; cloud still ON (Supabase URL baked in); Version history + "Retry now" intact.
- **Steps (SIGNED IN, on planyr.io):**
  1. Sign in. Open a site and add several **buildings** so the plan is materially bigger than its last cloud copy; wait for the header badge to read **"Synced вң“"**.
  2. **Hard-reload** (`Ctrl+Shift+R`) вҖ” several times вҖ” watching the canvas the instant it paints.
  3. **Expect:** it resumes **straight into the latest plan** (full building count) with **no flash of an older/thinner version first** and **no bounce to the map**. (The bug being fixed: a split-second older copy painted on load, then "came back on its own.")
  4. **"Disappears on its own" trigger:** switch to another tab for ~2вҖ“3 min, then return / refocus the Planyr tab вҶ’ still the latest plan, no flash, no bounce.
  5. **Two-source sanity:** if this device's local cache holds a thinner copy than the cloud, boot must still end on the **fuller merged** copy, never the thin one.
- **Expect:** at no point does an older / thinner plan appear, even for one frame; the resumed plan is always the newest merged copy. This is the **display half (cause #5)** of the persistence data-loss work.
- **If it fails:** **data-display class** вҖ” if an older plan still flashes or sticks on reload, record the exact step + the browser console + whether the badge read "Synced вң“" first, and flag it (don't log-and-move-on).
- **Cross-refs:** **V13 / V15** (the durability halves вҖ” B124 / B126, work must never actually disappear), **B134** (this fix's item вҖ” its causes #3/#4, work that never reaches any store, remain open), **B125** (the still-open honest save-status / `beforeunload` guardrail for that never-saved case), **B136** (the one-time SCHIEL recovery).
